              <tr>
                            <th>Team</th>
                            <th>Drives</th>
                            <th class="active up" colspan="2">TDs/Dr</th>

<div id="block-tableexplanationfreestatsnflmaindrivestats" class="block block-region-footer_outside block-type-table_info">
  <a class="table-info-trigger">
    <span>This table explained</span> <i class="fa fa-plus"></i> <i class="fa fa-minus" style="display: none;"></i>
  </a>
  <div class="table-info-content" style="display: none;">
    
        
          
            <div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-body field--type-text-with-summary field--label-hidden field__item"><p><em>Database updated: 12/08/2021 11:13 AM EST</em></p>
<p>These stats are computed from NFL Drive Charts and are not adjusted for strength of schedule or situation.</p>
<p><b>DSR</b>Â represents Drive Success Rate, as introduced inÂ <i>Pro Football Prospectus 2005</i>, which measures the percentage of down series that result in a first down or touchdown.Â <b>TO/Dr</b>Â represents turnovers per drive.Â <b>FUM/Dr</b>Â represents fumbles lost per drive.Â <b>LOS/Dr</b>Â represents average starting field position (line of scrimmage) per drive.Â <b>TOP/Dr</b>Â represents time of possession per drive.</p>
<p>Take-a-knee drives at the end of a half are discarded.Â <b>NET</b>Â values are simplyÂ <b>OFFENSE</b>Â minusÂ <b>DEFENSE.</b></p>
<p>Drive and pace stats are compiled by Jim Armstrong.</p>
</div>
